***proberen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:proberen.html>proberen</a> (434)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:proberen.html>proberen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to try, prove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">probāre</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">probō</i>.
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">problēma</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πρόβλημα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">próblēma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***question.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> question (161)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i>Zelfstandig naamwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b>question</b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:vraag.html>vraag</a>
<dl><dd>«I have a <b>question</b>.»
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vraag.html>vraag</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i>Werkwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b>question</b>
</p>
<ol><li>ondervragen</li>

***samen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:samen.html>samen</a> (295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tsamen</i>, a contraction of earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tesamen</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:samen.html>samen</a></i>. Although not clear from the spelling, the ⟨s⟩ in the Middle Dutch word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> pronounced as voiced <span class="IPA">/z/</span>. That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">(<a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:samen.html>samen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> pronounced <span class="IPA">/(tə)zaːmən/</span>, like the modern descendant <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tezamen</i> and the related words <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gezamenlijk</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">verzamelen</i>. The contracted form <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tsamen</i>, however, <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a voiceless <span class="IPA">/s/</span> because it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> assimilated to the preceding <span class="IPA">/t/</span>, creating an affricate. This affricate <span class="IPA">/ts/</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> simplified to <span class="IPA">/s/</span>.
</p><p>Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:samen.html>samen</a></i> derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">saman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*samana</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sem-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one, together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">sommige</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:soms.html>soms</a></i>, from the zero grade of the same Indo-European root.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:samen.html>samen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>together</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bijeen</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schuld</a> (516)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schuld</a></i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schout</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">skult</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skuldiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schuld</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schulden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schuldje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance<span class="ib-comma">,</span> accounting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> debt, account payable
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">vordering</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Vanwege <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> exorbitant hoge <b><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schulden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a>, besloot Annie <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Nigeriaanse prins <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> gijzelen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Because of the astronomically high <b>debts</b> he owed to her, Annie decided to take the Nigerian prince as a hostage.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> any obligor’s duty to perform
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">vordering</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>blame, fault <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">responsibility for a mishap or mistake</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> legde <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schuld</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> misdaad <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> wanbetaler.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She laid the <b>blame</b> for the crime on the one who failed to pay.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> guilt, culpability
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>Maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> hof <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> overduidelijk <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schuld</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">But the court <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> abundantly clear about her <b>guilt</b> of deprivation of liberty.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>guilt; fault <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">condition of moral deficiency</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>Door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schuld</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schuld</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schuld</a>!</b></i>
<dl><dd>By my <b>fault</b>, by my <b>fault</b>, by my most grievous <b>fault!</b></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***sinds.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a> (478)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sint</i>, with a suffix <i>-s</i>. The form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a nasal variant of Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sīþiz</i>, also found in Old High German <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">sint</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> According to some, <i>sint</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> instead shortened from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sīdent</i>, which itself <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> related with Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">siþþan</i> and Old Norse <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">síðan</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, however, improbable because <i>sint</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> already found in the oldest stages of both Dutch and German. Modern Dutch <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> therefore, in all likelihood, just an indirect cognate of the similar sounding English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">since</i>. The onset <i>s-</i> (instead of expected <i>z-</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to a prepositioned <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, thus <i>*<a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> zinds</i> → <i>*tzinds</i> → <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a></i>. Immediately cognate with Luxembourgish <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">zanter</i>. Also cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">seit</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">since</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>since
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">sedert</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">sindsdien</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Voorzetsel"><i>Voorzetsel</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li>sedert, vanaf <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a></b> vorige week in Rome.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i>Synoniemen</i></span></h5>

<div style="clear:both;"></div>

***slecht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a> (381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From an earlier meaning of “simple, ordinary, inferior, plain”, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">smooth, flat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sleht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slihtaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slechter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">slechtst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bad</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">ordinary</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">simple</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">common</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">mean</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>Heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:soort.html>soort</a></b> verloopstukken?</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> stichting <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:soort.html>soort</a> rechtspersoon.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>: <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(biologie)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> groep levende wezens <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> bepaald aantal kenmerken gemeenschappelijk <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> onderling voort <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> planten, onderdeel <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> geslacht

***staan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a> (273)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stâen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stān</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stāną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>staan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stand, to be upright
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>Dus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>stond</a></b> gisteren in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> supermarkt <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a>...</i> ― <span class="e-translation">So I <b><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> standing</b> in supermarket yesterday and then...</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be, to be placed or located
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In Holland <b><a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">In Holland there <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> a house.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zitten.html>zitten</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Forms a continuous aspect. Although it carries an implication of standing, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> vague and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not strictly required or emphasized.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sta.html>sta</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> koken?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What <b>are</b> you cooking there?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to say, to be written, to be said <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to be indicated in written form</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> grondwet <b><a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> kabinet verantwoordelijk <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> beleid <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> koning onschendbaar <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">In the constitution <b>it says</b> that the cabinet <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> responsible for governance and that the king <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> inviolable.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suit, fit, befit (of clothing)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It <b>suits</b> you!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***stad.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a> (375)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stat</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stedi</i> (whence <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stede</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stee</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stadiz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stéh₂tis</i>.
</p><p>The plural has preserved the old Germanic umlaut in a morphological function, a rarity in Dutch. Several derived terms have umlaut as well.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>steden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stadje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>city, town</li>
<li>the town/city centre
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I am now in <b>town</b>. I am now in the centre (of town).</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a></b> in.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I am going into <b>town</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***steeds.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a> (241)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stedes</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a></i>, an adverbial genitive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stede</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">steadfast, durable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with umlaut from the more common <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stade</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stādi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stēdi-</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">stets</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>always, continually, all the time, every time, each time
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He's working <b>all the time</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>increasingly, more and more, ever (+ <i>comparative</i>)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a></b> slimmer.</i>
<dl><dd>He's growing <b>increasingly</b> smart.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoppen.html>stoppe</a></i>.

***stuk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stuk</a> (520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stucke</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stuc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stukki</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stukkiją</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stück</i>, dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">steck</i> and borrowed <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shtick</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stuk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stuks</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stukje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>piece, item <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a thing, <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>ware</a>; often untranslated in English</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> peren vers? <a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stuks</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Are the pears fresh? Then give <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> four of them.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stuk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stukken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stukje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>piece, part <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a whole</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> snij <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> peer in <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stukken</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I’m cutting this pear in four <b>pieces</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">deel</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>play, skit</li>
<li>document (especially official)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hottie, babe, attractive person <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of any gender</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">erfstuk</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoofdstuk</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kerkstuk</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kopstuk</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>By shortening of the adverbial form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stuk</a></i>, now obsolete and superseded by <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stukken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pieces</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stuk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stukker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">stukst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>broken</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The adjective <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used chiefly predicatively. At least colloquially, however, inflected forms are quite common: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stukke</a> wasmachine</i> (“a broken washing machine”), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stukker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stuk</a></i> (“it’s totally ruined”, literally: “more broken than broken”).</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> support (150)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord_3"><i>Zelfstandig naamwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b>support</b>
</p>
<ol><li>draagvlak</li>
<li>steun
<dl><dd>«He <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <b>support</b> from the opposition.»

***te.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> (21)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>too <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">indicating excess</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>nooit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">too much <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> never good</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gek.html>gek</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">far out!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_3">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">modifying an infinitive verb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> something to eat</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>located at, in, on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a></b> Amsterdam</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">in Amsterdam.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> rijden <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> paard</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">and so <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> ride on horseback.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Article">Article</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> in idiom; a form of the definite article <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a> drommel</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">by Jove.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This preposition used to govern the dative case. It also fused with the dative forms of the definite article:
</p>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at, in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ter</span> = <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> + <span class="Latn" lang="nl">der</span> for feminine singular.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at, in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ten</span> = <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> + <span class="Latn" lang="nl">den</span> in all other cases.</li></ul>
<p>Combinations with the nominative form of the article, like *<i><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> or *<i><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i> have never become part of the language. The collapse of the inflection system and the related demise of the distinction between masculine and feminine gender (for most speakers) has pushed this preposition into partial disuse. It does however occur in a fair number of idiomatic expressions, often with fossilized case endings, e.g.:
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> elfder ure.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at the eleventh hour</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigen.html>eigen</a> bate</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for one's own profit</span></div></dd></dl>
<p>(<i>Elfder</i>, <i>ure</i> and <i>bate</i> are dative forms of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">elfde</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">baat</i> respectively.)
</p>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Voorzetsel"><i>Voorzetsel</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> plaatsaanduidingen: in.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> geboren <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> Amerongen.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> gebruikmaking <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>, per, middels.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>Komt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> voet, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> paard, <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> fiets?</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> vuur <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> zwaard bestrijden.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a> regelmatig <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> in combinatie <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> infinitief.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> beveel <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zitten.html>zitten</a>.</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vraag.html>vraag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>.</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> duidelijk <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<dl><dd>Vanouds <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <i><a href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/datief" class="extiw" title="w:datief">datief</a></i>. In <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> staande uitdrukkingen <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> bewaard <a href = vnd.unilang:blijven.html>gebleven</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> in samentrekkingen <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> lidwoord:
<dl><dd>ten = <a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></a> + den (<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>, <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>)</dd>
<dd>ter = <a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></a> + der (<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>)</dd></dl></dd></dl>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i>Bijwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li>in <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>grotere</a> mate of hoeveelheid <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> wenselijk <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> </i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:snel.html>snel</a><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a>, lukt <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tjegen</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> jegen</i>, the latter from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gegin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gagin</i>. </p>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> fiets <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deur.html>deur</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> of omstreeks <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> bepaalde <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a>

***terug.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a> (105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">rug</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">back</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zurück</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>backwards, back (in the opposite direction)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neem.html>Neem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> stap <b><a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> rechts.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Take a step <b>back</b>, and then go to the right.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>back, to a previous place or condition
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Give it <b>back</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>back, in return
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>Toen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> zwaaide, zwaaide <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">When my friend waved to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, I waved <b>back</b> at him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>again, back again
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>Toen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> donker <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>viel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:slapen.html>slaap</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">When she saw it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> still dark, she fell <b>back</b> asleep.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***tijd.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> (142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tijt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tīt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tīdiz</i>.

***toch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> (91)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></i>, alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">doch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>still, nevertheless, anyway
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ziek, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:werkt.html>werkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He's sick, but he <b>still</b> keeps working.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>after all, despite what <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> expected
<dl><dd><i>Ach, <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a>!</i>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>, you did come <b>after all!</b> [I thought you would not.]</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>yes, surely; <span class="use-with-mention">implies a positive contradiction, used to contradict a negative.</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>Wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> meekomen?  |  <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>Toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a>!</i>
<dl><dd>Don’t you want to come along?  |  <b>Yes,</b> I do!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">In positive statements, a modal particle indicating certainty or emphasis, implying that the speaker considers his statement to be obvious.</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> automonteur!</i>
<dl><dd>I wouldn’t know that! I’m no car mechanic!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">In questions, a modal particle indicating uncertainty or sometimes worry, implying that the speaker hopes to be confirmed or reassured; may also be postpositioned as a tag question.</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a>?</i> (with emphasis on <i><a href = vnd.unilang:gekomen.html>gekomen</a></i>)
<dl><dd>He <b>did</b> come, <b>didn't he</b>?</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>Jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> Gerrit, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a>?</b></i>
<dl><dd>You’re Gerrit, <b>aren’t you?</b></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i>Bijwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:gebruiken.html>gebruikt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> extra <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> benadrukken
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> rode broek <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> opvallend.</i> </li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tuo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tō</i>.

</p>

***toen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a> (121)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>doe</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a></i> (with <i>-n</i> from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thuo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þō</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">dunn</i> and similar forms (<i>do, du, dun</i>) in German dialects.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>then, subsequently <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">at a time in the past</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>Toen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><b>Then</b> he left.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>back then, at the time, in those days
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>Toen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewoon.html>gewoon</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><b>Back then</b> that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> still quite normal.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>when, at the time that <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in the past</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

***tot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> (117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tōte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tote</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">toti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to, until</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">tōte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to, until</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">until</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">zuo <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i>.
</p>

***tussen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a> (398)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tusschen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twisschen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tusschen</i>, a shortening of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">intwiskan</i>, originally a prepositional phrase <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*in twiskan</i>. The latter word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twiskaz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twiskijaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twofold, double</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dwís</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twice, doubly; in two</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> (135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twêe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">twē</i>, neuter form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">twēne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twai</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dwóh₁</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_2">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***u.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> (28)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally the accusative/dative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>gij</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">iu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*iwwiz</i>, West Germanic variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*izwiz</i>, dative/accusative of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jūz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yū́</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a></i>.
</p><p>The use as a nominative stems from an original possessive <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>uwe</a> edelheid</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">your nobility, your gentility</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> shortened to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a> E.</i> and finally to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">jo</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">jo</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">ju</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">you</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">euch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_7">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The capitalization of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i> (as in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a></i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>Uw</a></i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now considered old-fashioned, and no longer compulsory. In religious contexts, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still often capitalized, when addressing <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>.</li>
<li><i>See usage notes at</i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>gij</a></i>.</li></ul>

***uit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> (60)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">uut</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ute</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ūt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ūt</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">út</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">out</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">aus</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">ud</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>out, from the inside to the outside</li>
<li>out, off <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to an extinguished or switched-off state</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> vuur <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>The fire <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>out</b>.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> televisie <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>The television <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>off</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, finished, completely
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> spel <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>The game <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></b>.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> las <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> boek <a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>She read the book <b>completely</b>. (that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, to the very end)</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a> (306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ure</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hōra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uurtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>an hour, a period of time
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a>.</i>  |  She's coming in an hour.</dd></dl></li>
<li>the hour, the time of day
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>doe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wakker.html>wakker</a>?</i>  |  What are you doing still awake at this hour?</dd></dl></li>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The singular form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> normally used after numerals. Thus: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>vele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a></i> – for many hours; but: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a></i> – for three hours.
</p>

***uw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a> (119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*iuwa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*izweraz</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jouw.html>jouw</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a></strong> (<i>dependent possessive,independent possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>uwe</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>Second-person singular and plural</i>; your</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In standard Dutch this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the polite form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jouw.html>jouw</a></i>. However, in Flanders it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> commonly used as both formal and informal. The word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jouw.html>jouw</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not commonly used in Flanders. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>Uw</a></i> may merge  with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i> in some dialects and sociolects.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="NavFrame" style="float: left; width: 65em">
<div class="NavHead" style="background: CCCCFF;">Dutch personal pronouns</div>
<div class="NavContent">

</div></div>

</p>
</body> 
***vaak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> (512)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vake</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">often</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">faka</i>, dative singular of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">compartment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vak</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>frequent, regular</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vake</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">facon</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fag</i>.
</p>
