***van.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> (12)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fanē</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pone</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pana</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*apo-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pā-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">off, of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">fana</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">fan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">fan</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">fon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">fona</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">fon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a> (184)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fast</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fastuz</i>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a telephone</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> using a landline</li></ol>

***veel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> (114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>vele</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">filo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*felu</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">meest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>many, much, a lot of</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>As a determiner <i><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a></i> typically isn't inflected in informal Dutch. In formal style the inflected form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>vele</a></i> may be used, but only for plurals or before (usually uncountable) singular nouns with a definite article:
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>Vele</a></b> rolstoelgebruikers <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a> bezwaren <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> plannen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Many</b> wheelchair users <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> objections against the plans.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>vele</a></b> geweld dreef inwoners <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>large amount</b> of violence drove inhabitants away.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="3" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoeveel.html>hoeveel</a></span></li>

***vent.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vent.html>vent</a> (496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vent.html>vent</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hero; <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Unknown earlier origin. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">feint</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">servant; fellow; boyfriend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Fent</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">young fellow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<ul><li>Possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*fanþijō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">walker, walking</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pent-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go, pass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. This would make it related to Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to find; (archaic) to explore</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">fendo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">footsoldier</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fēþa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">footsoldier</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The expected descendant in Dutch would have been <i>vend(e)</i>, which existed in Middle Dutch as <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vende</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pawn in a chess game; farmer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Final_obstruent_devoicing" class="extiw" title="w:Final obstruent devoicing">Final-obstruent devoicing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> common in Dutch and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> already widespread in Old Dutch, rendering <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vent.html>vent</a></i> as a variant of <i>vend(e)</i> possible.</li>
<li>Possibly a shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vennoot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">partner (in a company)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> equivalent to a compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">veem</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(storage) company</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">genoot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">companion, partner</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no evidence of an overlap in senses.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vent.html>vent</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vent.html>venten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vent.html>ventje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>chap, fellow</li></ol>

***verdomme.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdomme.html>verdomme</a> (271)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The present singular subjunctive form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">verdommen</i>, likely an alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">verdoeme</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">verdoemen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to damn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdomme.html>verdomme</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>dammit!</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">verdorie</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">verdikke</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">verdikkie</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdomme.html>verdomme</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention"> singular present subjunctive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">verdommen</i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i>Werkwoord</i></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:verdomme.html>verdomme</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li>aanvoegende wijs <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> verdommen</li></ol>

***vergeten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a> (428)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vergēten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fargetan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*fragetan</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to forget <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">lose remembrance of</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naam.html>naam</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I’ve <b>forgotten</b> his name.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to forget <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fail to do</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deur.html>deur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> slot <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>forgot</b> to lock the <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to leave <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fail to take</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> sleutel <a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I’ve <b>left</b> my key at home.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>The perfect tenses of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></i> are predominantly construed with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i> for all senses, but the construction with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> equally common in the sense “fail to take”. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also somewhat common in the sense “fail to do”, but quite rare in the sense “lose memory of”.</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">  past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a></i></span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">findan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*finþaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pent-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go, pass; path, bridge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">after searching</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gevonden.html>Gevonden</a></b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Found</b> (it)!</span></div></dd>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find, to come across

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find, to think, to feel, to be of opinion
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> film walgelijk.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They <b>find</b> the film disgusting.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***voor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> (26)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vore</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vor</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fora</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fore</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furai</i>. There were originally two distinct Germanic forms, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furai</i> and <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furi</i>, which functionally merged in most Germanic languages, including Dutch. The form derived from the former became standard in Dutch, while the latter survives as the dialectal form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">veur</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>for</li>
<li>before</li>
<li>in front of</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voors</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pro, advantage, upside, positive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> overwoog <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He considered the <b>pros</b> and cons.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">pro</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">contra</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vore</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*furh</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furhs</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorbij.html>voorbij</a> (464)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vorebi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorbij.html>voorbij</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>past; just beyond</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">postpositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> past <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">implying motion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> rijd <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> stilletjes <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huisje</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voorbij.html>voorbij</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>And then don't quietly ride <b>past</b> our house.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vrâgen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">frāgon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*frēgōną</i>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to require, need

***vrij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a> (425)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">frī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*frijaz</i>, which derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*PreyH-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be fond of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vrijen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to love</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vrijdag</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">friday</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">friend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">woman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vrede</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">peace</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrijer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vrijst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>free; not imprisoned or enslaved.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">a free <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>free; unconstrained.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrije</a> hand <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a free hand <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>free; unobstructed, without blockages.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> (53)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wāer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*war</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwar</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">where</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> where, in which place
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>Waar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Jan?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Where</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> John?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> where, the place that
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> woont.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>where</b> he lives.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with a preposition</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> what, which thing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>Waar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>What</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that good for?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with a preposition</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> what, that which
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>what</b> that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> good for.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>With a preposition, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used instead of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></i> to create a pronominal adverb. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>See Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wâer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wār</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wēraz</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarheid.html>waarheid</a> (497)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">waerhede</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wārheit</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wārheid</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wārheide</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wērahaiduz</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
